31.1.16

[170]Echo Chamber Music

   Moose! Moose! Moose! Moose! Moose!
   Caboose! Caboose! Caboose! 'oose!
   Dialed the reverb down
   or do you prefer
   Moose! Moose! Moose! Moose! Moose!
   Caboose! Caboose! 'oose! Moose! Loose!
   Turned the echo off
   [171][Happy_moose.jpg]
   Credit: http://uncyclopedia.wikia.com/wiki/File:Happy_moose.jpg
   Posted by [172]Philip C James at [173]10:42:00

18.12.15

[538]Totemic Polemic

   Americans' Superheroes.
   Sorting the World's woes.
   Though hogs might fly,
   Before they'd cheer for Gun Control Guy.
   Or do you like
   America's Superheroes.
   Sorting the World's woes.
   The one Superhero bound to turn necks red?
   Background Checking Fed.
   [539][640px-Molon_labe.jpg]
   "Molon labe" by Fkerasar.
    Licensed under CC BY-SA 3.0 via Commons
   Posted by [540]Philip C James at [541]01:07:00
   Reactions:
